		completion_reward = {
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = JAP4_human_wave_doctrine
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_1
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = JAP4_establish_high_command
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_2
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = JAP4_never_ending_barrage
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_3
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_completed_focus = JAP4_blitzkrieg
				}
				add_ideas = RI_mobile_tactics_4
			}
			else = {
			    custom_effect_tooltip = RI_mobile_tactics
			}
		}
	}

		icon = GFX_goal_generic_construct_mil_factory
		x = 80
		y = 5
		cost = 10

		prerequisite = { focus = JAP4_night_vision }
    	prerequisite = { focus = JAP4_peoples_storm
                         focus = JAP4_peoples_officers }
		prerequisite = { focus = JAP4_combined_arms }
		
		completion_reward = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = arms_factory
										size > 0
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							dockyard > 0
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 2
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
					}
					any_owned_state = {
						is_coastal = yes
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_coastal = yes
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_effort_built
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = naval_effort_built }
					any_owned_state = {
						dockyard > 0
						free_building_slots = {
							building = dockyard
							size > 2
							include_locked = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						dockyard > 0

							building = dockyard
							size > 2
